<div id="review_1254405724" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1254405724" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1254405724?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24968581-fighting-silence">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1254405724" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14613942330901894762">First off. No one warned me this was going to be sad. You’re all assholes. Sure, everyone was like “You have to read this book, it’s sooooo good.” But not a single person warned me that it was going to cause my fucking eyes to leak. So for those reading this review, be prepared for a major case of the feels. Both happy and sad feels – but be ready to have this book take over your life while you’re lost within its pages.<br/><br/><a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/17023620307' title='Screenshot_20 by Book Worm, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429682181i/14620979.jpg' width='400' height='180' alt='Screenshot_20' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Till had one place he escaped to as a child. And one day that escape turn</span>
  <span id="freeText14613942330901894762" style="display:none">First off. No one warned me this was going to be sad. You’re all assholes. Sure, everyone was like “You have to read this book, it’s sooooo good.” But not a single person warned me that it was going to cause my fucking eyes to leak. So for those reading this review, be prepared for a major case of the feels. Both happy and sad feels – but be ready to have this book take over your life while you’re lost within its pages.<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/17023620307" title="Screenshot_20 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429682181i/14620979.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="Screenshot_20" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Till had one place he escaped to as a child. And one day that escape turned into a fantasy when a little girl is staring back at him. That was the first time climbing through a window changed his life, but it wasn’t going to be the last. Growing up poor, Till had nothing but his desire for more – more for his brothers, more for Doodle, more for everyone but himself. When he finds an afterschool program at the new gym that opened, Till’s about to get a chance at changing his future. But getting in the ring is the easy part. <br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/17229325932" title="Screenshot_2 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429682181i/14620980.jpg" width="400" height="256" alt="Screenshot_2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Eliza was without a family that showed her love her entire life. One boy changed that. She fell in love with the boy refused to use the door. And although that boy nearly broke her, but she couldn’t turn her back on the only person that ever made her feel like she had a family. <br>But one night months ago changed things for these two – for Eliza it gave her everything she always wanted, for Till though – it left him fearing his fantasy would fade and reality would steal everything away. But one thing stayed true. These two loved each other. When Till is forced to face the reality that his fighting career is going to be impacted by the loss of his hearing, he knows he has to continue on. All of this is for them – for Eliza for his brothers, to give them the life they deserve, a life that he can’t provide without the ability to fight. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/16608602814" title="Screenshot_1 by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429682181i/14620981.jpg" width="400" height="173" alt="Screenshot_1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I did not read the blurb before starting this, there were plenty of recommendations flying at me from all sides to know that I’d love this. So maybe I should have prepared myself a bit by reading it... I didn’t so imagine my surprise when Till drops the bomb that he’s going to lose his hearing... but that wasn’t all of it. It was the struggle he faced as he tried to provide a life to those he loved – by ensuring that he sacrificed everything so they didn’t have to. The loss of hearing her voice. The struggle of risking his fantasy for a reality, that right here kicked me in the feels big time. I was so heartbroken for him and yet willing to stand strong next to Eliza as she held her ground. <br><br>This love story was epic. <br><br>I had never read a book by this author and that is about to change. This is the type of book that has you crazy one-clicking after finishing. You just want to experience this author’s writing all over again. In the end, this book just hit all the marks. It was so well written, the depth of the characters was outstanding and the story was solid and unique. A highly emotional read that although had you in tears for the sadder times, made you cry happy tears when you got your ‘best’ moments. I fell hard for Till and can’t wait to get lost in the prior books from this author and get my needy hands on the next in the series.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14613942330901894762" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1205110701" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1205110701" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1205110701?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1205110701" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12176073255225527055"><b>FOUR PAGE BROTHERS STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"... claim me. I’ll claim you too."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453460946i/17829535._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Have I found a new author to claim as a favourite? I think that is what has just happened right here. Aly Martinez has got me wrapped up in her writing and I may have just experienced the crazy feelings that go alongside a monumental book hangover. Why you may ask? It's all down to this authors gorgeous writing talent and it has to be said that this book right here is phenomenal. <br/><br/><b>What's it all about?</b><br/>This is the first book in the 'on</span>
  <span id="freeText12176073255225527055" style="display:none"><b>FOUR PAGE BROTHERS STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"... claim me. I’ll claim you too."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453460946i/17829535._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Have I found a new author to claim as a favourite? I think that is what has just happened right here. Aly Martinez has got me wrapped up in her writing and I may have just experienced the crazy feelings that go alongside a monumental book hangover. Why you may ask? It's all down to this authors gorgeous writing talent and it has to be said that this book right here is phenomenal. <br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>This is the first book in the 'on the rope' series and it sets the stage for the Page brothers to make their debut into our reading hearts. Till page is the eldest of the three brothers and to call him a born survivor is an understatement. These brothers face hardship and difficulties and with a heart breaking past and tragic circumstances following their every move they have to fight hard to find their happiness. This book takes the reader on the unmistakable journey of finding hope and love. Aly Martinez takes the tried and tested method of a friends to lovers theme but there's nothing unoriginal here. Follow the story of Till Page and the love of his life and best friend Eliza Reynolds and hold on to your seats for a love story that is memorable to say the least. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453460946i/17829536._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>Those who know me will be able to tell you that my favourite of all tropes to read in the romance reading world is the friends to lovers story. I love the angst, the anticipation and the feeling of desperation for the perfect twosome to finally realise that they can't live without falling in love with each other. So it comes with no surprise that I fell hard in love with this story. Aly Martinez takes this trope and makes it her own, it's so much more than friends falling in love. This, my fellow readers is about soul mates finding their match. If I was to choose an author for a weepy, soul searching story I would always navigate towards Martinez, this author has a way of delivering the emotions but making sure her readers are rewarded with a heart pounding romance and love that is nothing short of epic. <br><br><b>Why not five?</b><br>Aly Martinez is new to me as an author and to say I'm impressed would be an understatement. If this book is anything to go by then you can be rest assured that I won't be missing out on future releases. This book was definitely a weeper, it was packed full of hardships and difficulties and whilst I was impressed with the quality of story telling I did at times feel like I wanted more peaceful story telling of the characters lives. The beginning had me hooked, but as the story developed I found myself a little on the distracted side. But these are only small niggles, I loved this authors voice and I'm more than ready to grab ahold of book two in the series. A solid four star rating for a book that was beautifully and thoughtfully put together.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453460946i/17829537._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>A fantastic start to a series that is sure to capture the hearts of the reading community. I can't wait for more in the series to come and I'm glad that I listened to the voice of my fellow romance addicts and gave this book a try. Well worthy of your time and money spent, don't miss out on this gorgeous love story. You won't regret it for a minute. Enjoy ... Kisses. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12176073255225527055" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1176041262" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1176041262" />
    <a title="Vanessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12059859-vanessa"><img alt="Vanessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576765878p2/12059859.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1176041262?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vanessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vanessa" href="/user/show/12059859-vanessa">Vanessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYBODY!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=super-steamy">super-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=kick-ass-heroines">kick-ass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=heavy-emo-reads">heavy-emo-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=stay-with-you-reads">stay-with-you-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=auto-buy-authors">auto-buy-authors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1176041262" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13076393932079138546"><b>
  <i>6 The Silencer STARS!!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/Fighting%20Silence%20Casting_zpsfjfxakfp.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424899284i/13817233._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo Fighting Silence Casting_zpsfjfxakfp.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She burst out laughing. God, I loved that sound so much. I knew I’d never be the same when I lost it to the silence. I’d happily give up every noise in the world if I could just keep her laugh. But my life didn’t work that way.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><i>Spoiler Free Review</i><br/><br/>Just WOW!!!<i>Fighting Silence</i> is one of those rare books that only comes along every once in a while that you just have to experience to understand. This was my first read by this author and I was completely blo</span>
  <span id="freeText13076393932079138546" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>6 The Silencer STARS!!!!</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/Fighting%20Silence%20Casting_zpsfjfxakfp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424899284i/13817233._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Fighting Silence Casting_zpsfjfxakfp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She burst out laughing. God, I loved that sound so much. I knew I’d never be the same when I lost it to the silence. I’d happily give up every noise in the world if I could just keep her laugh. But my life didn’t work that way.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Spoiler Free Review</i><br><br>Just WOW!!!<i>Fighting Silence</i> is one of those rare books that only comes along every once in a while that you just have to experience to understand. This was my first read by this author and I was completely blown away! <br><br>This is the <b>BEST</b> Contemporary Romance read I have picked up in a loooong time! Well over a year. I have actually been going darker and grittier lately, just because this genre was falling flat for me. <br><br>Basically, Eliza and Till meet when they are kids. They've both been dealt a pretty crappy hand in life. They have total shit parents who don't give a crap about them, and they come from very little. They become best friends, hidden away in an abandoned apartment near where they both live. This story spans about 8 years of their lives. It's a friends-to-lovers tale and an EPIC-ALLY beautiful one at that!! <br><br>I will not give away anything about the plot. In fact, go in as blind as you can here so that you can experience the beauty that is this book, spoiler-free! Till and Eliza both have different outlooks on their circumstances. Whereas as Eliza is ever the optimist, Till recognizes that everything in his reality is pretty much shit, except for Eliza, so he keeps her in what he calls his fantasy world. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Till and I both knew we had a strange relationship. It was more than a friendship, but there wasn’t romance or sex. There was definitely love though. Immeasurable amounts of it. I knew that Till had this grand fantasy about me."<br><br>“I can’t have you without claiming you for forever.” “Then claim me. I’ll claim you too.”<br><br>“I want it all,” he whispered, licking his lips before continuing. “Every single first you have to give, I want it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/Reality20is20a20prison_zpshqxg5h0y.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424905512i/13818236.jpg" alt=" photo Reality20is20a20prison_zpshqxg5h0y.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But over the years, they go from friends, to pretty much family, to more. This particular element of the book reminded me a bit of the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13372690.Slammed__Slammed___1_" title="Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Slammed</a> series, by Colleen Hoover in that, Eliza and Till are pretty much raising Till's two younger brothers, Flint and Quarry. And OMG, did I LOVE these boys!!!! The author does a simply magnificent job of blending in the secondary characters just enough into the story to where I totally fell in love with them too!! My heart really broke for Till. This amazing guy worked himself to the bone to give his brothers the best life he could. <br><br>And let me just stop for a minute to say that Eliza should win some kind of damn award for being the most fierce and kick ass heroine EVER!!! What a strong woman! I had just as big of a girl crush on her as I did on sexy ass Till, and Flint, and Slate...haha!! Till is the external force of strength in the book while she in the quiet, internal one. And even though it is Till that gets in the ring every day, they are both fighters. She's strong, sexy, determined, and funny. And Till is determined, loving, protective, and humble. Just loved them both. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Truth be told, I’d have been happy to sit in an empty room for the rest of my life as long as he was sitting beside me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/8901672_zpsh2oxyhwr.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424906203ra/13818318.gif" alt=" photo 8901672_zpsh2oxyhwr.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And oh boys and girls, the love story!!!!! ALL THE FEELS!!! Heart pounding, goosebumps. I can honestly say, there is not one single thing that I did not LOVE about this book! And what made it completely stand apart from the rest for me is that, again, NO STUPID DRAMA!!! Not even for a second! Nothing annoyed me... which is pretty rare, let me tell you! Eliza and Till deal with everything that comes at them like a solid unit in this book. I absolutely love books where we get to watch the H/h enduring and growing <u>together</u>. (Granted, they are not a couple for the whole time. They are "friends" for a while, but still.) And HOT!!! Yeah, fret not, there is plenty of scorching steam in this one!!! &lt;3 <br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/9253689ab8e3649e76c6aff8ff237dc8_zpsd7o1bxxv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424905512i/13818237.jpg" alt=" photo 9253689ab8e3649e76c6aff8ff237dc8_zpsd7o1bxxv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Sometimes, in the world we lived in, where everything was a struggle, it was easy to become dependent on the things that numbed the chaos. Some people turned to drugs or alcohol as an escape. But I had Till . . . and he had the fantasy."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't know what else to say except for that, books like these are the reasons that I read!!! The reason that I stay up until 4 am, when I have to be up at 7 (like I did here), chasing that magical feeling that only a truly amazing book can give me. <br><br>So grab a box of tissue (because you will need it), hunker down, and ENJOY!!! Once I started this book, it was completely impossible to put down!<br><br>And OH THAT ENDING!!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/06c789a769e4efdb6628dd7dbbeedc3f_zpshbqzmkge.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424904545i/13818122.jpg" alt=" photo 06c789a769e4efdb6628dd7dbbeedc3f_zpshbqzmkge.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/c15c1ca572a9256b481fc9b077e90772_zpszp1chafv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424905920i/13818267.jpg" alt=" photo c15c1ca572a9256b481fc9b077e90772_zpszp1chafv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved it so much, that I am jumping into Slate's book next, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21951329.Among_the_Echoes__Wrecked_and_Ruined___2_5_" title="Among the Echoes (Wrecked and Ruined, #2.5) by Aly Martinez" rel="nofollow noopener">Among the Echoes</a>. Which by the way, you can totally read that series before, after, or not at all, and still read and love this book. <br><br><i>Fighting Silence</i> is book 1 in a series of stand alones following the Page brothers. I CANNOT wait for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23206498.Fighting_Shadows__On_the_Ropes___2_" title="Fighting Shadows (On the Ropes, #2) by Aly Martinez" rel="nofollow noopener">Fighting Shadows</a> next, which will be Flint's book!!! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If it means you guys are taken care of, I will sit in silence for the rest of my fucking life.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/Fighting%20Silence%20Collage_zpsdxgvnddf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424907758i/13818485._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Fighting Silence Collage_zpsdxgvnddf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1209959082" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1209959082" />
    <a title="Jayme" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29482055-jayme"><img alt="Jayme" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1400069469p2/29482055.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1209959082?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jayme" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jayme" href="/user/show/29482055-jayme">Jayme</a>
      </span>

I heard a lot of good things about this book, so when I had the chance I started to read without hesitation. And I wasn't disappointed.   <span id="freeText8159775377090457725" style="display:none">Yeah, yeah... I just set in the line of the Page brothers fan club. I heard a lot of good things about this book, so when I had the chance I started to read without hesitation. And I wasn't disappointed. You also won't be.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455032756i/18045950._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>About the plot:</b> Eliza and Till met at the age of thirteen. They both came from families with problems, who were not interested in their children. They both ran away from them and hid in an abandoned apartment in their neighborhood. This is where they met, and where continued and developed their friendship. They were everything to each other and their bond was very strong.<br><br>Together growing up their friendship changed, they began to meet with new difficulties. Only those moments in deserted place were their shelter and escape from reality. Especially for Till. So when Eliza want to go forward and started to build their future, he went crazy. Everything has complicated and their friendship was put to the test. <br><br><b>Final thoughts:</b> It is so beautiful and moving book. And even though we know a lot of friends to lovers stories, it was very unique and had a refreshing plot. It can be funny and touching. It can be sexy and romantic. It is simply everything.<br><br>I very much like the character of Eliza. She was soft and strong at the same time. She was able to stand up, take responsibility, first for yourself, then for her new family. Because she not only had to cope when Till had doubts, but also with his younger brothers, who, besides their two do not have any other authority. I just love the the bond that they have together, four of them as family.<br><br>Till is something else. His desire to be able to escape from reality could frustrate, but he was a fighter and fought with all his heart. And he has a really big and wonderful heart. Even when he struggled with his progressive hearing loss. Always his heart was full of love for Eliza and his brothers. He gave us a lot swoon worthy moments and crocodile tears.<br><br>Although it already is a lot, it's not the end of story, there's more. They have a lot of challenges in front of them all the time. And when Till begins to fight in the professional ring, and their financial situation is improving, there are always difficulties and different problems. But in family strength, and together they will fight to the end. They found strength in between the ropes and in love. It's beautiful and inspiring, like this whole book. Never stop fighting and absolutely read it. <br><br>***<b>Quick Review:</b>***<br><br><b>Series: </b> The first in the On the Ropes series. <br><b>Grade/Tag Tabs: </b> New Adult. Sports Romance.<br><b>Release Date: </b> February 23rd 2015<br><b>Main characters: </b> Eliza Reynolds, Till Page. The characters grow up during the course of the story. They met as 13 year olds and the action takes many years to adulthood. They both come from families with problems. Eliza likes to draw, then study accounting. He caught a lot of jobs until had a chance to become a professional boxer. <br><b>Secondary characters: </b> Absolutely amazing Page brothers, Flint and Quarry. <br><b>Location: </b> Indianapolis.<br><b>Steamy:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes. Sexual tension is high, and there are several hot scenes.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Sensitive topic: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes. Violence. Disability.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Love triangle:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Not exactly, but they had other relationships in the meantime. The book takes on a space of several years.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cliffhanger: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Next in the series?</b> Yes. Book Two, <i>Fighting Shadows </i>, about Flint Page.<br><br><b>If I'd recommend?</b> Yes. Especially if you enjoy childhood friends to lovers touching stories about fighters with some angst and sensitive topics.<br><br>***<br>Follow me on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JaymeBooks-677210922331986" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> or <a href="https://twitter.com/Jayme_Books" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>. <div id="review_1197907517" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1197907517" />
    <a title="Snow" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31719636-snow"><img alt="Snow" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465808156p2/31719636.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1197907517?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Snow" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Snow" href="/user/show/31719636-snow">Snow</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=5-star-read">5-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=fighters">fighters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=disability">disability</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=na">na</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1197907517" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4755938668035937656"><br/><b>6 "The Silencer" stars</b><br/><br/><b>FIGHTING Silence</b> is the first book in the <b>„On the ropes series“</b> and <b>MY first book</b> by <b>Aly Martinez.</b><br/><br/>I am glad I finally got to it. <b>This story was remarkable.</b> It drove me into the world where fictional characters collide with the reality and you can't help but getting involved to the maximum. Feeling and experiencing with them. Being emotionally engaged in the story leaves you quite exausted in the end but it makes you very much alive and vivid.<br/><br/>There aren't absolutely no objec</span>
  <span id="freeText4755938668035937656" style="display:none"><br><b>6 "The Silencer" stars</b><br><br><b>FIGHTING Silence</b> is the first book in the <b>„On the ropes series“</b> and <b>MY first book</b> by <b>Aly Martinez.</b><br><br>I am glad I finally got to it. <b>This story was remarkable.</b> It drove me into the world where fictional characters collide with the reality and you can't help but getting involved to the maximum. Feeling and experiencing with them. Being emotionally engaged in the story leaves you quite exausted in the end but it makes you very much alive and vivid.<br><br>There aren't absolutely no objections to the development of the story, characterisation or the flow of the words in the book that I can think of and justify with arguments. It's perfect in dealing with human imperfections as an aspect of life and powerfull in the detailed presentation of the everyday struggle. <br><br>The obstacles are all around us, sometimes smaller, sometimes bigger, sometimes even impossible at first sight BUT they are rarely given to us in everyday life without a reason even if we are not the ones to know it at the given moment or we may never find the reason or any sense or any answer to „why“ it happened.<br><br>So <b>this story</b> is just a <b>wessel to show that „fights“ are a constant, life is a fight, literally or metaphorically BUT it's a struggle, it's a 50:50 chance in winning or losing, and you can look at it as a <i>„glass half full“</i> of a <i>„glass half empty“</i> manner , that is up to you, BUT even in that option no one is actually truly alone.</b><br><br><b>Till Page and Eliza Reynolds</b> are the <b>main characters</b> in this <b>story of surviving the odds, of winning the life's wheel of fortune, fighting against the wrong cards dealt in life, against circumstances, against the unjust laws of nature, fighting for your place in the WORLD, in this LIFETIME.</b><br><br>They both come from dysfunctional families and they find each other at the tender age of 13 in an abandon appartment. Entering the window, which will mark Till's perception of safety, shielded environment later on, he encounters Eliza, talented girl with a scatch pad and aload of loneliness on her shoulder. They find refuge in each other forming a bond and finding things in common while creating their own safe bubble of solace, comfort and deep friendship. This friendship grows deeper and deeper through out the years and when the time for Eliza's departure upon graduation comes they find another level of love in each other. <br>The passion of young love discovered out of pure need for solace and belonging.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I want it all… Every single first you have to give, I want it.”<br>… “Then they’re all yours,”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1454095647p8/1383230.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"There were hands, mouths, and tongues. Fingernails raking his skin and his hand in my hair. Slow glides followed by deep thrusts.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But the overwhelming notion that their safe little world has been breached and is threatened by the clutches of the real world that is waiting for them, takes them apart for awhile, basically cause Till feels he's inadequate to give Eliza what she needs and deserves. So he feels the right thing to do is to leave her. BUT while they struggle each with their own reality and obligations, the destined path brings them back together again.<br><br>Their friendship never ended only the physical aspect of attraction lingers above them and while Eliza is ready to take it upon her and make it real, Till is the one that is holding himself back being afraid of what the cruel reality can do to them.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I can’t give her what she wants!”<br>“Pull your fucking head out of your ass and stop being such a pussy. You living in this ridiculous ass fantasy world is fucking up reality for the rest of us. Including her.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Till is holding the <b>„fantasy“ of their safe world of untouchable and ideal close to him</b> and he's very much <b>struggling within himself</b> to keep in line with his obligations to his two younger brothers that he had to provide for and take care of since they were left by their unworthy mother and criminal father. He's working non-stop, trying to provide for them all, bring food on the table, struggling each day with the lack of money, frustration of lingering dreams of better, and the cruel truth that sets him for miles back as the <b>merciless silence is pending above him while he slowly loses his sense of hearing.</b><br> <br>He's devastated and lost and his anger is pouring out. But what Till didn't count for is Eliza. Eliza who was there. EVERY STEP OF THE WAY. For good, bad and worse. She was his rock, partner, link, bond. <b>She was his forever.</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I love you, Eliza Reynolds, and if I had my way, I’d lock you up in a room and keep you all for myself. But if you insist on doing that whole ‘living a real life’ thing, I want to go with you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Even with knowing how young they both were, the love they felt for each other was believable, palpable and I swallowed each breath they took while expressing it. I believed them in every word spoken, every motion made, every glimpse, every tiny little atom of their affection was imbeded into my soul. And that alone was the true anchor that got me stuck forever</b><br><br>Together, <b>Till and Eliza embraced the cruel fact of disability that was imposed into their lives and they turned it around, they owned it and made it work. They faught with each breath, touch, word to support each other, to comfort, to heal, to sooth and make it bearable, make it real, their real.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1454095584p8/1383227.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Till let go of the <b>„fantasy“</b> by accepting the <b>„reality“</b>. By closing the window and opening the door to start the <b>new reality – their reality.</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“With one sentence and two steps, forever began. Till Page walked through my door for the very first time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>He gets the chance to <b>box professionally</b> that would enable him to provide more for his family and he takes it. AND just for the sake of it, the life turned its ugly face again and imposed it's claws once more…BUT Till and Eliza made it again inspite of all negativity, inspite of the ugly past that came to haunt and hurt them, inspite all the odds…<b>they made it.</b> cause <b>they belong.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1454094904p8/1383221.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There is nothing in this world that was ever more mine than you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1454095613p8/1383228.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Phenomenal story with so much depth in revelation and thought and emotions that cut you deep, to the bone</b>. They sink deep into your core of your inner being and make you so completely phased by the notion of what actually matters in life. <b>That notion makes you humble and aware of the small things that are truly important.</b> That truly each and every one of our lives is made of. <b>That „reality“ is worth fighting and living for.</b><br><br><b>ONE OF THE BEST STORIES I HAVE READ THIS YEAR</b><br><br><b>BR with my fighter doll, Lady D (aka Denise)! *wink*<br><br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4755938668035937656" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1202706514" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1202706514" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1202706514?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=series-book">series-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=sports-theme">sports-theme</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=mma-romance">mma-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=march-2015">march-2015</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1202706514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13828955289402662978">Every so often a book comes around that speaks to your soul, and captures your full attention. That is what "Fighting Silence" did for me. I adore this book, absolutely; adore it! Yes, there is sex in it, and romance, as well as all the gushy stuff we like; but beyond that is a story of two kids who were from homes where they were pretty much ignored; found one another and made life the best that it could be. They did this together, and eventually they created a family out of what they were give</span>
  <span id="freeText13828955289402662978" style="display:none">Every so often a book comes around that speaks to your soul, and captures your full attention. That is what "Fighting Silence" did for me. I adore this book, absolutely; adore it! Yes, there is sex in it, and romance, as well as all the gushy stuff we like; but beyond that is a story of two kids who were from homes where they were pretty much ignored; found one another and made life the best that it could be. They did this together, and eventually they created a family out of what they were given; which wasn't much. At a young age they both ended up with Till's younger brothers to take care of too, and even with so little; they had what was the most important...and that is LOVE.<br /><br />So, as usual...I tend to get ahead of myself!! The hero and heroine in this book, begin with meeting in an abandoned apartment at the age of thirteen. Till Page is a boy who has the weight of the world on his shoulders, and the biggest challenge he will eventually face is going deaf in the future. With such a grim prognosis, and a crappy home life to boot; reality doesn't feel much like a place he likes to be in all the time. On top of all of that, his parents are losers, and his younger brothers end up getting most of their security from Till himself. I'm not kidding when I say this guy has the weight of the world on his shoulders. My heart bled for him. The day he climbs through a window and finds thirteen year old Eliza Reynolds sitting in an abandoned room, is the day his life changes forever...and both of them meet their soul mate. Eliza also has a lot on her plate, and her parents basically ignore her. We don't get a lot of info into her home life; but from what I gathered...she was sort of left to find her own way in the world. When Till Page waltzes through that window, she finds her future family.<br /><br />I was amazed how these two were able to pull together at such a young age, and be responsible, loyal, and determined. They truly had the secret to family in my opinion...because when the challenges came, instead of taking things out on each other; they worked together and faced things holding on to one another. Does that mean they didn't have times when they reacted wrong, and made poor choices? Of course not, they were young and human, and both Till and Eliza had their moments; but when the chips were down..they were there for one another always. Once Till's brothers came into the picture, I truly fell in love with all of the characters involved. I loved how having each other made them all stronger. There is also a sports aspect to this book as well, and the Page brothers all end up visiting the boxing arena. The owner of the Boxing place plays a very big role in all three of their lives.<br /><br />Bottom line, this is a must read story. I highly recommend it. It has heart...and I really did love every minute of it. The good,the bad, and the ugly! I took it all in; because hey....isn't that life?! We all go through major challenges, and usually come out the other end stronger for what we have endured. For Till and Eliza, this is nothing short of true. I fell in love with these characters; and the author did a beautiful job of writing them. She made them come alive before my eyes, and I won't ever forget The Page family! I'm glad to find out that there will be two more books in this series..because the two brothers were impossible not to fall in love with either! Bring it on, and here is yet another brilliant author to add to my growing list of favorites! Thank you Aly Martinez for writing such an intense story about my most favorite subject.....FAMILY!♥ </span>
  <a data-text-id="13828955289402662978" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>I'm not sure what took me so long to read <b>Fighting Silence-</b> . There's tons of glowing reviews for this books, reviews that are well-deserved, I might add! Typically I'm hit or miss with the New Adult genre. I can take a fair amount of drama but it needs to be the angsty kind and not immature. THIS is the kind of New Adult reads I love! It has all the elements of that first time at young love- coupled with a fair amount of strife yet hope- and bucket loads of angst f</span>
  <span id="freeText9396880994894167119" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 Angsty Awesome Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-05/C9B34540-280E-45D7-8115-904AC928D2EE_zpslgsj25uf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432763929i/15004807._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo C9B34540-280E-45D7-8115-904AC928D2EE_zpslgsj25uf.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I'm not sure what took me so long to read <b>Fighting Silence-</b> . There's tons of glowing reviews for this books, reviews that are well-deserved, I might add! Typically I'm hit or miss with the New Adult genre. I can take a fair amount of drama but it needs to be the angsty kind and not immature. THIS is the kind of New Adult reads I love! It has all the elements of that first time at young love- coupled with a fair amount of strife yet hope- and bucket loads of angst for good measure. Perfect! <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Till </b>and <b>Eliza </b>met in grade school. Not really friends, but classmates. Until one day Till climbs through an abandoned apartment window looking for a bit of solace. What he found was Eliza. Both 13-year old kids finding peace and quiet away from the hell of their home life. Escape. Fantasy. Years pass and their friendship and connection grows within their special haven. Till struggles to be a student, work two jobs to pay the rent his mother doesn't pay, and feed his two younger brothers. Until one day he notices a new gym in town. Boxing. Can he afford to add one more thing to his never-ending responsibilities? Could this pay off in his future?<br><br><br><i>
  <b>I had already been drowning in the ocean of life. Every gasp of air was a struggle. Just as I would breach the surface, filling my lungs with hope and determination to make it through another day, I was forced back under- harder every time.</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I really connected with this story is so many ways. The author did a perfect job displaying the hardships of urban life, especially with parents suffering through issues of their own. Kids end up raising their siblings just to put food in their bellies- the ADC checks going towards drugs and alcohol. It wasn't overdone. It was realistic. The connection between Till and Eliza was a slow build without the unrealistic insta-love. It was true and honest and Till only wanted the best for his Eliza. He just didn't realize right away that HE was what's best for her.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-05/EBBEFB15-CA3C-4C17-94C4-E56700254E77_zpsxzpz25wl.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432772284i/15005426._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo EBBEFB15-CA3C-4C17-94C4-E56700254E77_zpsxzpz25wl.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>That's about all I'm giving away of the plot. Read and experience the young love story that is Till and Eliza. Two young adults borne from squalor, facing life struggles, but with love and family, anything can happen if you set your sights on it. <br><br><br><b>"I love you, Eliza."<br>I relaxed as he very gradually filled me.<br>There were fireworks.<br>Stars.<br>Every possible cliche I could conjure.<br>No. It was <i>him.</i><br>We were young and reckless. <br>There was no condom.<br>Or discussion.<br>There were hands, mouths, and tongues.<br>Fingernails raking his skin and his hand in my hair.<br>Slow glides followed by deep thrusts.<br>Desperation. <br>Comfort.<br>There was Till.<br><i>And Eliza.</i></b><br><br>Yah...enough said from me.<br><br>Looking forward to Flint's book <b>Fighting Shadows,</b> out this summer. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427351718i/14265304.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

He I believe was not a virgin, but he wasn't sleeping around either. He did take her virginity, and said ILY, but he was also scared of moving forward their relationship because she was going to college and he didn't want to bring her down. He failed a couple classes and wasn't graduating. Later in the book when they are both adults, she gives him an ultimatum you can come through the front door (literally, it was symbolic too) or you have to let me go. She eventually tries to move on (sorta, it's half assed) and goes on a date with a guy and has a kiss. Also prior to their 1 time sleeping together, it also seemed to imply that SHE too had been with other guys, but again we don't get details, we don't get angst we don't get anything like that. So to me there wasn't cheating. AT ALL</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />So for this person (and the majority of romance readers) this isn't cheating. For me it is.<br /><br />However I'll still read this one day because a friend recommended it to me, so it'll be my stepping out my comforzone book. One day.<br /><br /><br />To my dear friends who don't mind OW or OM, I have read amazing reviews of this one, so don't let my non-review prevent you to read a book you might enjoy more. <br /><br /><br /><b>Note:</b> For the purpose of my reviews whatever activity with OW meaning kissing, trying to f@ck her, taking her to a hotel (even if later hero regrets it and "can't stop thinking about the heroine", watching her naked counts as disloyalty and cheating <b>IF( and only IF) </b>THIS HAPPENS AFTER H and h get together,. I consider they're together once they have exchanged a kiss even if there's no promise of exclusivity. If it is before they kiss I have no problem, but if it's after they have kissed I hate it. It makes the Hero weak and childish.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1203547017?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1203547017" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3709721796892236497"> <b>"I wanted to go home. But home wasn’t where I laid my head every night. I didn’t actually live there at all, but it was the only place I felt alive. What I needed was the dream that only existed inside those four walls."</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426086413i/13972103.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Fighting Silence is a beautiful love story about overcoming the darkness in life. It is a story of a boy and a girl struggling through the depths of poverty. Eliza and Till grew up in the same neighborhood. Till an awkward boy with dirty jeans and Eliza an artist whose parents </span>
  <span id="freeText3709721796892236497" style="display:none"> <b>"I wanted to go home. But home wasn’t where I laid my head every night. I didn’t actually live there at all, but it was the only place I felt alive. What I needed was the dream that only existed inside those four walls."</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426086413i/13972103.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fighting Silence is a beautiful love story about overcoming the darkness in life. It is a story of a boy and a girl struggling through the depths of poverty. Eliza and Till grew up in the same neighborhood. Till an awkward boy with dirty jeans and Eliza an artist whose parents have discarded her. Till and Eliza find security in the arms of each other. They share a tender friendship and begin to carry each other through the hardships of life. They provided for each other. Although they are only friends, in their hearts they both know that it is so much more. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426088546i/13972466.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Eliza cannot understand why Till goes out of his way to avoid her at school and yet clings to her every night in their secret haven.<br><br> <b>"See, Eliza Reynolds flew under the radar. Very few people at school knew who she was , and I intended to keep it that way. If she caught the attention of the football team, she’d be flooded with dates. So I ignored her at all costs so as to not draw any attention her way. I couldn’t risk that someone would take her away from me."</b><br><br>Till finds an after school boxing program where he is finally given mentorship from the gym owner. Eliza continues to study and work hard so that she can get into college and escape the confines of her parents. The night of Eliza's graduation Till finally shows Eliza how he feels for her. <br><br><b>“I can’t have you without claiming you for forever.” “Then claim me. I’ll claim you too.”</b><br><br>After that night, Till leaves her. He thinks he is doing the right thing by giving her a life with out him. She is distraught and left broken.<br><br>As the fates would be, Till is thrown into a violent situation. When it is done, he knows what he needs. He needs Eliza.<br><br><b>"I’d never had anything I could call my own, but Eliza Reynolds would always be mine." </b><br><br>Eliza is hesitant to let Till back in. They find even ground as friends. They begin to rebuild the brokenness that had occurred between them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426086413i/13972105.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>"Till and I both knew we had a strange relationship. It was more than a friendship, but there wasn’t romance or sex. There was definitely love though . Immeasurable amounts of it." </b><br><br>Meanwhile, Till's mom has bailed on his younger brothers. Till takes his younger brothers in to raise. The family dynamic that is born is beautiful, funny, heartbreaking, and unforgettable.<br><br> <b>"And that was the way we worked. We picked on each other relentlessly and laughed unabashedly. They fought. I refereed. It was perfect, really. We were a family."</b><br><br>As the story progresses, the questions continue to build in the background. Will Till be able to realize it's ok to be with Eliza? Will Eliza give up on waiting for him? Will they ever be able to break the chains of poverty? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426086413i/13972106.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On top of everything going on in this story (poverty, young love, family, boxing), Till is facing a serious medical condition. Although it is not life threatening, the results could alter his life forever. And it's important to mention, the condition is hereditary. The knowledge that it could pass down to one of his brothers is absolutely heart breaking. <br><br> <b>"Things would never go back to the way they were before, but we were all busy forging a new path with the life we had been handed. Sometimes it sucked, but, as a family, we never focused on that for too long." </b><br><br>What did I love about this story? Truthfully- everything! The plot was thick and yet unraveled neatly and naturally. The dual POV gave us a glimpse of both of these characters. Although Till's actions were somewhat frustrating at times, the choices and actions of Till only made me admire Eliza that much more. This heroine is one of a kind! The romance was tender as it developed from friends, to young love, to forever love! The love that Till and Eliza had for the boys was a testament to how love truly conquers all. This unique family was able to overcome poverty and create a beautiful life together! I simply cannot say enough about this book. It was phenomenal and I certainly will be checking out the next book in the series. If you are looking for a beautiful story that will leave you warm and fuzzy, this is the read for you!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426086413i/13972104.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>
  <a data-text-id="3709721796892236497" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1205434598" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5315744085565878737"><br/><b>RATING: 4.5 "...Ever more mine." Hearts!! :D <3 <3</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455771039i/18147982.png' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“With one sentence and two steps, forever began. Till Page walked through my door for the very first time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><i>Fighting Silence</i> beautifully reminds us of all the reasons we love the new adult genre, making us live and breathe with our compellingly complex characters so we’re subjected to each of their sharpest of pains and their warmest of joys. The synopsis of this leads us to believe we’ll find a mere best friends to lovers story, what </span>
  <span id="freeText5315744085565878737" style="display:none"><br><b>RATING: 4.5 "...Ever more mine." Hearts!! :D &lt;3 &lt;3</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455771039i/18147982.png" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“With one sentence and two steps, forever began. Till Page walked through my door for the very first time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>Fighting Silence</i> beautifully reminds us of all the reasons we love the new adult genre, making us live and breathe with our compellingly complex characters so we’re subjected to each of their sharpest of pains and their warmest of joys. The synopsis of this leads us to believe we’ll find a mere best friends to lovers story, what we uncover instead is the culmination of a romance that embodies the very essence of love, life, friendship, family, sacrifice, and struggle—an all-consuming, memorable combination in this first installment.<br><br>Eliza is someone who is easy to root for from the first page, her optimism in face of life’s big and little squalls and the fact that she’s been completely in love with Till Page her entire life but has found herself relegated time and again to the best friend role making our hearts hurt instantly. She’s unafraid to put her foot down when she’s had enough of Till’s back and forth however, instead she tells him exactly what she’s thinking and feeling and refuses to remain a fantasy when reality of a future with him is just a hairsbreadth from their reach. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I can’t have you without claiming you for forever.”<br>“Then claim me. I’ll claim you too.”<br>“That’s exactly what I’m afraid of, Eliza.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The romance between them is delicately stunning, an innocent friendship that grows into unequivocal love bringing a tension so thick we practically have trouble breathing as we read yet when the sparks fly we can’t help feeling the beginning rustle of butterfly wings in our bellies. Even though Till makes the start of their relationship difficult with his fear of losing her and even when they face a series of unfortunate events, their romance is nothing short of beautifully hopeful and heart-wrenching at the same time. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I was okay. <br>She was okay. <br>We were okay. <br>Nothing else matters.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>One other highlight that must be mentioned is Till’s younger brothers, Flint and Quarry, both of whom provide a light comfort with their interventions and leave much potential for their own stories. Overall, <i>Fighting Silence</i> creates in us a tangled mess of conflicting emotions until Ms. Martinez takes pity and leaves us with a smile on our faces, infused with the warmth that comes from experiencing a well-deserving couple get what they’ve always wanted. <br><br><br><u>Other Fav Quotes:</u><br><br><b>
  <i>“I want it all,” he whispered, licking his lips before continuing. “Every single first you have to give, I want it.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Posted: February 17, 2016</i>
</b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1209125453?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sabrina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sabrina" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina">Sabrina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1209125453" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13763299843431016471"><b>3 'Doodle' Stars</b><br/><br/>I liked this story, but it didn't wow me. My main issue was how much time the story kept skipping, and overall the whole book was over this wide time span. It made it seem like nothing was happening since it would skip forward a certain amount of time and then spend a few pages summarizing what happened in those weeks/months/years that we didn't see. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458849097ra/18539429.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>With that being said, I really did enjoy this book even with the few issues I had with it. I thought Eliza was an amazing character</span>
  <span id="freeText13763299843431016471" style="display:none"><b>3 'Doodle' Stars</b><br><br>I liked this story, but it didn't wow me. My main issue was how much time the story kept skipping, and overall the whole book was over this wide time span. It made it seem like nothing was happening since it would skip forward a certain amount of time and then spend a few pages summarizing what happened in those weeks/months/years that we didn't see. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458849097ra/18539429.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With that being said, I really did enjoy this book even with the few issues I had with it. I thought Eliza was an amazing character, and I loved how sweet she was. Usually I don't like the overly lovey, nice girls. But with Eliza it made the book interesting, and she was hilarious with Till, their witty banter had me laughing like a loon.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458849097ra/18539430.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bottom line, yes I had some issues with the way the book skipped over so much time, but I still liked the story and characters. This was my first book by Aly Martinez but it will definitely not be my last, I need to continue with this series! </span>
  <a data-text-id="13763299843431016471" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
