<div id="review_1155573136" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1155573136" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515708587p2/10367112.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1155573136?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=sports-romance">sports-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=loved-it">loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=sports">sports</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1155573136" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer740253705634853326"><i> ARC provided by author in exchange of honest review</i><br/><br/><a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/16419566589' title='#FS by ms.meesh, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424557368i/13777183.jpg' width='500' height='356' alt='#FS' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Every reader has an author who is an instant one-click and Aly Martinez is that author for me. And in her newest release, Fighting Silence, she has literally left me speechless. I am utterly in awe of this brilliant and emotional book that exposes the vulnerability, strength, and heart of what it truly means to be a FIGHTER. A fighter is known for its physical strength but a true fighter knows that it means nothing if you don’t have dedicat</span>
  <span id="freeText740253705634853326" style="display:none"><i> ARC provided by author in exchange of honest review</i><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/16419566589" title="#FS by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424557368i/13777183.jpg" width="500" height="356" alt="#FS" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Every reader has an author who is an instant one-click and Aly Martinez is that author for me. And in her newest release, Fighting Silence, she has literally left me speechless. I am utterly in awe of this brilliant and emotional book that exposes the vulnerability, strength, and heart of what it truly means to be a FIGHTER. A fighter is known for its physical strength but a true fighter knows that it means nothing if you don’t have dedication and can make sacrifices for your craft. And most importantly a true fighter must have HEART. The heart and belief that there is something worth fighting for. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/16430769369" title="#FS1 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424640751i/13786857.jpg" width="333" height="500" alt="#FS1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Fighting Silence is not your ordinary fighter romance book because Aly took her readers on an emotional and breathtaking tale of what it means to FIGHT. To fight for yourself. To fight for your family. To fight for your dreams. And the most importantly to FIGHT FOR LOVE. When you have the love and support of the most important people in your lives, nothing and no one can hold you back regardless of your social status. Aly Martinez didn’t just give us fictional characters, she gave us characters who inspire us to have HOPE and sometimes fantasy can become reality. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/16430769459" title="#fighting by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424640751i/13786858.jpg" width="460" height="500" alt="#fighting" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When you have to grow up so fast and take responsibility at a young age, reality can look bleak when you grew up on the wrong side of the tracks. At a young age, Till Page had to grow up so fast and become the man of the household when he had two neglectful parents, who should be providing the roof and food on the table. But for Till he became the breadwinner of the family. He is a testament of a boy who became a man instantaneously when he took the sole responsibility of the welfare of his two younger brothers, Flint and Quarry. When you live a life, where money is a struggle, dreams of a better future can look slim for a young man who doesn’t have a college education. But in the face of adversity, light and hope came in the form of Eliza Reynolds. The girl who took his heart from the moment he laid eyes on her when he was 13 years old. She was his fantasy. The one who owned his heart and made him feel like the richest man in the world.<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/16591085596" title="#fight2 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424643842i/13787157.jpg" width="500" height="405" alt="#fight2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Eliza and Till had this connection and bond that could not be destroyed. Their love and devotion to each other literally took my heart. There aren’t enough words to describe how touching and emotionally connected these two were. There love went beyond the words that Aly wrote because action speaks louder than words and their love was felt in every page. Every unspoken word, touch, tears shed and physical connection, the words of love, hope, family, sacrifices, and reality were FELT. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/15996936623" title="#fightin2 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424641511i/13786956.jpg" width="500" height="327" alt="#fightin2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Though this book was about love, dreams and reality, the underlying theme of FAMILY was predominant in the storyline as well. Till was not only a sweetheart and amazing hero, but he was also a brother and father figure to his younger brothers. Not many men would take on the sole responsibilities of the welfare of their younger siblings at a young age. Till was not only fighting for his dreams but he was fighting for the future for Flint, Quarry, and Eliza. He wanted to make sure the doors were open wide for the people he loved. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/16615786691" title="#Fighting3 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424642914i/13787088.jpg" width="500" height="330" alt="#Fighting3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/16431469229" title="#fight3 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424645171i/13787243.jpg" width="500" height="480" alt="#fight3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Fighting Silence is one of those books that must be experienced and read. It is a book that takes you on a journey of rediscovering of what truly matters in life. You can have money, fame, and glory but would that really make you happy in life when you don’t have the people you love with you. This is definitely a book that I will cherish and love because Aly Martinez truly captured my heart with this beautiful, heartbreaking, and uplifting tale. Fighting Silence is a reminder that one day we will find a place where our dreams and reality collide. What can I say but FIGHTING SILENCE IS A MUST READ!!!!<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/16617298351" title="#FS2 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424653617i/13788182.jpg" width="500" height="417" alt="#FS2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Teasers/f850f66983e102a20a1876a49cde93_zpstmvn0dma.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446783023i/16898539.gif" alt=" photo f850f66983e102a20a1876a49cde93_zpstmvn0dma.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> Review can also be found on Four Chicks Flipping Pages: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://fourchicksflippingpages.weebly.com/">http://fourchicksflippingpages.weebly...</a> </i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7374424.Aly_Martinez" title="Aly Martinez" rel="nofollow noopener">Aly Martinez</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="740253705634853326" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aZI3eOEnoVMYfFd5TIbVbrAWJDjy7HmdacS6voi1tqpHEuuDqeLmUDaNJrNaYZCwyMgt28FdD2TQHPO03yfuQQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Z62Ke/RpSndVHXymFBv4iSCZEICrQyEyvngyQjgWzlhJLVaAvKwNdHvsDWwC/L1XWEcZY5jyV8sHoHtIb4SWsw==')})
  }
